                context 'successful; A midgame.' do
        
      736.

          1
          
                  it 'midgame_with_no_moves' do
        
      737. 
      
        
    737. 
          1
          
                    game = FactoryBot.create(:midgame_with_no_moves, callback_wanted: :midgame_with_no_moves)

          1
